## Section C: Hijack-Word Leaderboard

Title words that appear most frequently in mismatch rows (across all BFCs).
A high count means the word is likely pulling SKUs into the wrong family.

> **Example from user report:** A SKU titled **"CHURRO TRAIL MIX"** in BFC
> *Popcorn, Peanuts, Seeds & Related Snacks* was routed to `Bakery > Pastry > Churros`
> instead of `Snack`. The word *churro* hijacked it via a title-regex rule.
> Below is the empirical count of how often each word appears in a mismatched title.
